\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l02748}02748\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Kurtosis\ is\ the\ fourth\ central\ moment\ divided\ by\ the\ square\ of\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l02749}02749\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ variance.\ If\ Fisher's\ definition\ is\ used,\ then\ 3.0\ is\ subtracted\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l02750}02750\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ the\ result\ to\ give\ 0.0\ for\ a\ normal\ distribution.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l02751}02751\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l02752}02752\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ If\ bias\ is\ False\ then\ the\ kurtosis\ is\ calculated\ using\ k\ statistics\ to}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03078}03078\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03079}03079\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Samples\ quantile\ are\ defined\ by\ \`{}\`{}Q(p)\ =\ (1-\/gamma)*x[j]\ +\ gamma*x[j+1]\`{}\`{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03080}03080\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ where\ \`{}\`{}x[j]\`{}\`{}\ is\ the\ j-\/th\ order\ statistic,\ and\ gamma\ is\ a\ function\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03081}03081\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}j\ =\ floor(n*p\ +\ m)\`{}\`{},\ \`{}\`{}m\ =\ alphap\ +\ p*(1\ -\/\ alphap\ -\/\ betap)\`{}\`{}\ and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03082}03082\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}g\ =\ n*p\ +\ m\ -\/\ j\`{}\`{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03083}03083\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03084}03084\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Reinterpreting\ the\ above\ equations\ to\ compare\ to\ **R**\ lead\ to\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03085}03085\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ equation:\ \`{}\`{}p(k)\ =\ (k\ -\/\ alphap)/(n\ +\ 1\ -\/\ alphap\ -\/\ betap)\`{}\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03086}03086\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03088}03088\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ (0,1)\ \ \ \ :\ \`{}\`{}p(k)\ =\ k/n\`{}\`{}\ :\ linear\ interpolation\ of\ cdf}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03092}03092\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ (0,0)\ \ \ \ :\ \`{}\`{}p(k)\ =\ k/(n+1)\`{}\`{}\ :}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03093}03093\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ (**R**\ type\ 6)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03095}03095\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ (**R**\ type\ 7,\ **R**\ default)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03096}03096\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ (1/3,1/3):\ \`{}\`{}p(k)\ =\ (k-\/1/3)/(n+1/3)\`{}\`{}:\ Then\ p(k)\ \string~\ median[F(x[k])].}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03097}03097\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ The\ resulting\ quantile\ estimates\ are\ approximately\ median-\/unbiased}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03228}03228\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ (0,1)\ \ \ \ :\ \`{}\`{}p(k)\ =\ k/n\`{}\`{},\ linear\ interpolation\ of\ cdf\ (R,\ type\ 4)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__mstats__basic_8py_source_l03229}03229\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ (.5,.5)\ \ :\ \`{}\`{}p(k)\ =\ (k-\/1/2.)/n\`{}\`{},\ piecewise\ linear\ function}}
